load('Final_Model_Predictions.mat')

Y = Predictions.Ytest;
models = {'LR','SVR','RF','ANN','LSTM'};

RMSE = zeros(5,1);
MAE  = zeros(5,1);
R2   = zeros(5,1);

for i = 1:length(models)
    Yp = Predictions.(models{i});
    RMSE(i) = sqrt(mean((Y - Yp).^2));
    MAE(i)  = mean(abs(Y - Yp));
    R2(i)   = 1 - sum((Y - Yp).^2)/sum((Y - mean(Y)).^2);
end

Results = table(models',RMSE,MAE,R2, ...
    'VariableNames',{'Model','RMSE','MAE','R2'});
save(fullfile(DIR.tables,'Final_Model_Results_Extended.mat'),'Results');
writetable(Results, fullfile(DIR.tables,'Final_Model_Results_Extended.xlsx'));
